# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
VirtualBox Network Adapters: Complete Guide ^1knfd0PE

Virtual Network Modes:
1. Not attached 
2. NAT
3. NAT Network
4. Bridged Adapter
5. Internal Network
6. Host-only Adapter
7. Generic  ^f9bAX7oT

Objectives:
virtual machines must be able to connect to physical and virtual networks with their virtual network adapters. 
Virtual machines running on VirtualBox can be connected to different networks. 
VirtualBox provides multiple network modes for virtual machines. ^1uMQ8C9V

with these adapter, we can able to connect with multiple networks on each machines. 
Each VirtualBox VM can use up to eight virtual network adapters, 
each of which in turn is referred to as a network interface controller (NIC).

Each virtual network adapter can be separately configured to operate 
in a different network mode. ^hxCyHi4Y

Virtual Network Adapters:

A virtual network adapter is a software-emulated physical device. 
There are six virtual adapter types that can be virtualized by VirtualBox.

VirtIO networking drivers are a part of the KVM project and are open-source. T
hese drivers are available forLinux with kernel 2.6.25 or later, and Windows 
including older versions such as Windows 2000, XP and Vista. ^yvy1ggVf
